Many times used in real estate transactions, its terms are based primarily on the worth of the property being used as security, not on the credit reliability of the borrower.\r\n\r\n$ Payday loans - A payday loan (also called a payday advance, early salary loan, payroll loan, small dollar loan, short term, or cash advance loan) is a small, short-term unsecured loan, “regardless of whether repayment of loans is linked to a borrower’s payday.” \r\n\r\n$ Peer to peer lending - Peer-to-peer lending, also abbreviated as P2P lending, is the practice of borrowing money and lending money to individuals or businesses through online services that match lenders with borrowers.
